21–22 Point Pioneer Decks from Players Tour Brussels 2020












21–22 Point Pioneer Decks
-------------------------


The players of the following decks got seven match wins and a draw out of the ten Pioneer rounds.








#### Garcia Gonzalez, Sergio - Dimir Inverter


#####
